Here is a sample questionnaire on Stress at work:

**Stress at Work Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
Thank you for taking the time to participate in this survey. Your responses will help us better understand the stress levels and factors contributing to stress at work. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to elaborate on your responses if you'd like.

**Section 1: Demographics**

1. What is your current job title?
_____________________________________________________
2. How many years have you been working at [Company Name]?
_____________________________________________________
3. What is your department/ team?
_____________________________________________________

**Section 2: Stress Levels**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how would you rate your current stress levels at work (1 = very low, 5 = very high)?
_____________________________________________________
2. Have you experienced increased stress levels at work over the past 6 months? (Yes/No)
3. Have you ever experienced a burnout or felt exhausted from work? (Yes/No)

**Section 3: Causes of Stress**

1. Which of the following work-related factors causes you the most stress? (Select up to 3)
	* Lack of control over tasks or decisions
	* Unrealistic workload or expectations
	* Conflicting priorities or deadlines
	* Limited resources or support
	* Other (please specify) _______________________
2. Do you feel that your workload is manageable? (Yes/No)
3. Are there any specific tasks, projects, or situations that cause you stress? If yes, please describe.
_____________________________________________________________________

**Section 4: Coping Mechanisms**

1. How do you typically cope with stress at work? (Select all that apply)
	* Take regular breaks
	* Practice deep breathing or meditation
	* Engage in physical activity
	* Talk to a colleague or supervisor
	* Seek professional help or counseling
	* Other (please specify) _______________________
2. Have you noticed any changes in your coping mechanisms over the past year? (Yes/No)
3. Are there any new coping mechanisms you'd like to try or have tried in the past that were helpful?

**Section 5: Suggestions for Improvement**

1. What would you suggest to reduce stress levels at work? (Open-ended question)
_____________________________________________________________________
2. Are there any specific policies, procedures, or resources you think would be helpful in managing stress?
_____________________________________________________________________

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to participate in this survey. Your input is invaluable in helping us understand the stress levels and factors contributing to stress at work. If you have any additional comments or suggestions, please feel free to include them below.

_____________________________________________________________________

**Workplace Environment Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
Thank you for taking the time to participate in this survey. Your input will help us understand the current state of our workplace environment and identify areas for improvement. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to provide additional comments or suggestions as needed.

**Section 1: Overall Satisfaction**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how satisfied are you with the overall work environment in our company?

1 (Very Dissatisfied) to 5 (Very Satisfied)

2. What do you like most about our workplace environment?

(Open-ended text field)

3. What do you like least about our workplace environment?

(Open-ended text field)

**Section 2: Physical Workspace**

4. How would you rate the cleanliness and organization of your workspace?

1 (Poor) to 5 (Excellent)

5. Do you have a dedicated workspace that meets your needs?

Yes / No / Sometimes

6. Are there any physical workspace issues that affect your productivity or comfort? If yes, please describe.

(Open-ended text field)

**Section 3: Communication and Collaboration**

7. How would you rate the effectiveness of communication within our team?

1 (Poor) to 5 (Excellent)

8. Do you feel encouraged to share your ideas and opinions with your colleagues and superiors?

Yes / No / Sometimes

9. Are there any communication or collaboration challenges that you face regularly? If yes, please describe.

(Open-ended text field)

**Section 4: Work-Life Balance and Well-being**

10. How would you rate your work-life balance?

1 (Poor) to 5 (Excellent)

11. Do you feel supported in your well-being and mental health by your employer?

Yes / No / Sometimes

12. Are there any work-related factors that affect your well-being or stress levels? If yes, please describe.

(Open-ended text field)

**Section 5: Feedback and Suggestions**

13. Do you have any suggestions for improving our workplace environment?

(Open-ended text field)

14. Is there anything that you would like to see changed or improved in our workplace environment?

(Open-ended text field)

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to participate in this survey. Your input is invaluable in helping us create a better workplace environment. If you have any additional comments or suggestions, please feel free to include them below.

(Open-ended text field)

Let me know if you'd like me to make any changes or if you're ready to convert this questionnaire into a specific format!

[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a questionnaire on Remote Working Experience:

**Introduction:**
As part of our ongoing efforts to improve our remote work policies and procedures, we would like to gather your experiences and insights on working remotely. Your input will help us create a better working environment for everyone. Please answer the questions honestly and to the best of your ability.

**Section 1: General Remote Work Experience**

1. How often do you work remotely?

a) Daily
b) 2-3 times a week
c) 1 time a week
d) Less than once a week
e) Rarely

2. What is your preferred remote work setup?

a) Home office
b) Co-working space
c) Coffee shop or library
d) Other (please specify)
e) I prefer to work in the office

3. How would you rate your overall experience working remotely?

a) Very positive
b) Somewhat positive
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat negative
e) Very negative

**Section 2: Productivity and Focus**

4. Do you find it easier or harder to stay focused and productive while working remotely?

a) Easier
b) Same
c) Harder

5. What are some common distractions you face while working remotely? (Select all that apply)

a) Family members or roommates
b) Social media
c) Email notifications
d) Phone notifications
e) Other (please specify)

6. Do you have a dedicated workspace for remote work? If so, what is it like?

a) Yes, it's quiet and comfortable
b) Yes, it's noisy or distracting
c) No, I work from a shared space or public area

**Section 3: Communication and Collaboration**

7. How do you prefer to communicate with colleagues and managers while working remotely?

a) Video conferencing (e.g., Zoom, Google Meet)
b) Phone calls
c) Email
d) Instant messaging (e.g., Slack, Microsoft Teams)
e) Other (please specify)

8. Have you experienced any challenges with communication or collaboration while working remotely? If so, how did you overcome them?

9. Do you feel like you're missing out on important information or updates while working remotely?

a) Yes
b) No
c) Sometimes

**Section 4: Work-Life Balance**

10. Do you find it easier or harder to maintain a healthy work-life balance while working remotely?

a) Easier
b) Same
c) Harder

11. How do you prioritize self-care and take breaks while working remotely?

12. Do you have any concerns or suggestions for improving work-life balance while working remotely?

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to share your thoughts and experiences on remote working. Your feedback is invaluable in helping us create a better remote work environment.

[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a sample questionnaire on End of working relationship:

**End of Working Relationship Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
The purpose of this questionnaire is to gather feedback and insights on the end of working relationships within our company. Your responses will help us understand the reasons behind the termination of employment, the effectiveness of our exit process, and areas for improvement.

**Section 1: Reasons for Termination**

1. What was the primary reason for the termination of employment? (Select one)

a) Performance issues
b) Lack of job fit
c) Company restructuring
d) Voluntary resignation
e) Other (please specify)

2. Were there any underlying factors that contributed to the termination? (Check all that apply)

a) Poor communication
b) Lack of training or support
c) Conflicting goals or priorities
d) Unfavorable work environment
e) Other (please specify)

3. Did the employee receive any formal warnings or counseling prior to termination? (Yes/No)

**Section 2: Exit Process**

1. How would you rate the overall effectiveness of our exit process? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "ineffective" and 5 is "very effective")

2. Were the employee's expectations met during the exit process? (Yes/No)

3. Did the employee receive all necessary information and support during the exit process? (Yes/No)

**Section 3: Managerial Support**

1. How would you rate the support provided by the manager during the termination process? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "ineffective" and 5 is "very effective")

2. Were there any communication breakdowns or misunderstandings during the termination process? (Yes/No)

**Section 4: Recommendations for Improvement**

1. What changes or improvements would you suggest to enhance our exit process?

2. Are there any additional resources or support that would have been helpful during the termination process?

**Section 5: Additional Comments**

1. Is there anything else you would like to share about the end of working relationship?

2. Are there any suggestions or recommendations for improving our company's overall employee retention and engagement?

Thank you for taking the time to provide your feedback. Your input is invaluable in helping us improve our processes and support our employees.

Please note that this is just a sample questionnaire, and you can modify it according to your specific needs and goals.
     - User:

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a sample questionnaire on Onboarding:

**Onboarding Experience Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
Thank you for taking the time to participate in this survey! Your input will help us understand the onboarding experience of new employees and identify areas for improvement. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to provide any additional comments or suggestions you may have.

**Section 1: Pre-Onboarding Experience**

1. How did you first learn about the job opening at our company?

a) Job posting on our website
b) Referral from a current employee or friend
c) Job fair or recruitment event
d) Social media or online job board
e) Other (please specify)

2. Did you receive any information about the company culture or values before starting?

a) Yes, I received an email or brochure
b) No, I didn't receive any information
c) I received some information, but it was limited

3. Were you prepared for the onboarding process before your first day?

a) Yes, I felt well-prepared
b) Somewhat prepared, but had some questions
c) Not very prepared, and had many questions

**Section 2: Onboarding Process**

1. How would you rate the overall onboarding experience?

a) Excellent
b) Good
c) Fair
d) Poor

2. Which of the following best describes your onboarding process?

a) Formal orientation with HR and management
b) Informal introduction to colleagues and supervisor
c) Online training or tutorials
d) Combination of the above

3. Did you receive a comprehensive onboarding packet or guide?

a) Yes, it was very helpful
b) Yes, it was somewhat helpful
c) No, I didn't receive one

**Section 3: Support and Feedback**

1. How would you rate the level of support you received during your onboarding process?

a) Excellent
b) Good
c) Fair
d) Poor

2. Did you receive regular check-ins or feedback from your supervisor or HR?

a) Yes, it was very helpful
b) Yes, it was somewhat helpful
c) No, I didn't receive any

3. Were you encouraged to ask questions or seek help during the onboarding process?

a) Yes, I felt encouraged
b) Somewhat encouraged, but had some hesitation
c) Not very encouraged, and felt hesitant to ask questions

**Section 4: Additional Comments**

1. What did you like most about the onboarding process?

2. What did you like least about the onboarding process?

3. Do you have any suggestions for improving the onboarding process?

4. Is there anything else you'd like to share about your onboarding experience?

Thank you for taking the time to complete this survey! Your input is invaluable in helping us improve the onboarding process for future employees.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Onboarding

[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a sample questionnaire on Manager Feedback:

**Manager Feedback Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
As part of our ongoing efforts to improve management practices and employee development, we would like to gather your feedback on your experiences working with your manager. Your input will help us identify areas of strength and opportunity for growth. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to provide additional comments or suggestions.

**Section 1: Managerial Style and Communication**

1. How would you rate your manager's overall communication style?

a) Clear and concise
b) Somewhat clear, but could improve
c) Not very clear
d) Not at all clear

2. Does your manager regularly provide feedback on your performance and goals?

a) Yes, always
b) Mostly, but not always
c) Rarely
d) Never

3. How would you rate your manager's ability to listen and respond to your concerns?

a) Excellent
b) Good
c) Fair
d) Poor

**Section 2: Leadership and Guidance**

4. How would you rate your manager's leadership and guidance in achieving your goals and objectives?

a) Strongly supports and guides
b) Somewhat supports and guides
c) Doesn't provide much guidance
d) Doesn't support or guide

5. Are you satisfied with the level of autonomy and independence your manager gives you to make decisions?

a) Very satisfied
b) Somewhat satisfied
c) Neutral
d) Dissatisfied

6. How would you rate your manager's willingness to take calculated risks and try new approaches?

a) Encourages and supports
b) Somewhat encourages and supports
c) Doesn't encourage or support
d) Discourages and doesn't support

**Section 3: Employee Development and Growth**

7. How would you rate your manager's support for your professional development and growth?

a) Strongly supports and encourages
b) Somewhat supports and encourages
c) Doesn't support or encourage
d) Doesn't care or support

8. Are you satisfied with the opportunities your manager provides for learning and skill-building?

a) Very satisfied
b) Somewhat satisfied
c) Neutral
d) Dissatisfied

9. How would you rate your manager's ability to recognize and reward your achievements and contributions?

a) Excellent
b) Good
c) Fair
d) Poor

**Section 4: Additional Comments and Suggestions**

10. Is there anything your manager does exceptionally well that you would like to see continued or expanded?

11. Are there any areas where your manager could improve or provide more support?

12. Do you have any suggestions for how your manager could better support your growth and development?

b) Somewhat encourages and supports

**Training to Professional Users Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
As part of our ongoing efforts to improve our training programs, we would like to gather your thoughts and opinions on your training experiences. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to provide any additional comments or suggestions you may have.

**Section 1: Current Training Practices**

1. How often do you participate in training sessions or workshops?
	* Daily
	* Weekly
	* Monthly
	* Rarely
	* Never
2. What types of training do you typically attend? (Select all that apply)
	* Technical skills training
	* Soft skills training (e.g., communication, leadership)
	* Industry-specific training
	* Compliance training
	* Other (please specify)
3. What motivates you to participate in training sessions? (Rank in order of importance)
	* Professional development and growth
	* Compliance and regulatory requirements
	* Company expectations and policies
	* Personal interest and curiosity
	* Other (please specify)

**Section 2: Training Satisfaction**

1. How satisfied are you with the overall quality of training provided by our organization?
	* Very satisfied
	* Satisfied
	* Neutral
	* Dissatisfied
	* Very dissatisfied
2. How relevant are the training topics to your current job responsibilities?
	* Very relevant
	* Somewhat relevant
	* Not very relevant
	* Not at all relevant
3. Have you noticed any improvements in your job performance or skills as a result of training?
	* Yes
	* No
	* Unsure

**Section 3: Training Challenges**

1. What are the most significant challenges you face when it comes to participating in training sessions? (Select all that apply)
	* Scheduling conflicts
	* Limited time availability
	* Lack of relevance to job responsibilities
	* Inadequate training materials or resources
	* Other (please specify)
2. Have you ever felt that a training session was not effective or relevant to your needs?
	* Yes
	* No
	* Unsure

**Section 4: Training Preferences**

1. What format do you prefer for training sessions? (Select all that apply)
	* In-person classroom training
	* Online webinars or virtual training
	* On-the-job training or mentoring
	* Self-paced online learning
	* Other (please specify)
2. How important is it for you to have opportunities for hands-on practice or application of new skills?
	* Very important
	* Somewhat important
	* Not very important
	* Not at all important

**Section 5: Additional Comments**

1. Do you have any suggestions for improving our training programs or services?
2. Are there any specific training topics or areas you would like to see addressed in the future?

Here's a sample questionnaire on Employee Potential:

**Employee Potential Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
The purpose of this questionnaire is to assess your potential as an employee and identify areas where you can grow and develop within the company. Your feedback will help us understand your strengths, weaknesses, and interests, and inform our talent development and succession planning initiatives.

**Section 1: Personal and Professional Background**

1. What motivates you to come to work every day?
	* Please select one or more: (e.g., sense of accomplishment, helping others, learning new skills, etc.)
2. What are your greatest strengths, and how do you utilize them in your current role?
3. What are your greatest weaknesses, and how do you work to improve them?
4. What are your long-term career goals, and how do you see yourself growing within the company?

**Section 2: Job Satisfaction and Engagement**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how satisfied are you with your current job?
	* 1 (very dissatisfied) to 5 (very satisfied)
2. What aspects of your job do you enjoy the most, and why?
3. What aspects of your job do you find most challenging, and how do you overcome those challenges?
4. How often do you feel energized and motivated by your work?

**Section 3: Learning and Development**

1. What skills or knowledge do you wish you had to improve your performance in your current role?
2. How do you prefer to learn new skills or knowledge: through formal training, on-the-job experience, or online resources?
3. What opportunities would you like to have to develop your skills and advance your career?
4. Are there any specific areas where you would like to receive training or mentorship?

**Section 4: Leadership and Management**

1. Do you see yourself in a leadership or management role in the future? Why or why not?
2. What qualities or skills do you think are essential for effective leadership?
3. Have you had any formal leadership or management training? If so, what was the most valuable takeaway?
4. How do you prioritize and delegate tasks to achieve your goals?

**Section 5: Feedback and Suggestions**

1. What feedback would you like to receive from your manager or peers to improve your performance?
2. Are there any changes or initiatives you would like to see implemented within the company to support employee growth and development?
3. Is there anything else you'd like to share about your potential or areas for growth?

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to complete this questionnaire! Your input is invaluable in helping us understand your potential and identify opportunities for growth and development within the company.

**Course Feedback Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
We value your opinion and want to hear about your experience in the [Course Name]. Your feedback will help us improve the course and provide a better learning experience for future participants. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to provide additional comments or suggestions.

**Section 1: Overall Satisfaction**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how satisfied are you with the course overall? (1 = Very Dissatisfied, 5 = Very Satisfied)

2. What did you like most about the course?

3. What did you like least about the course?

**Section 2: Course Content**

4. How relevant was the course content to your needs and expectations?

5. Were the learning objectives clearly stated and achievable?

6. Were the topics covered in the course well-organized and easy to follow?

7. Were there any topics or areas that you felt were missing or underemphasized?

**Section 3: Instructional Methods**

8. How effective were the instructional methods used in the course (e.g., lectures, discussions, hands-on activities)?

9. Were the instructors knowledgeable and engaging?

10. Were the pace and tempo of the course suitable for your learning style?

**Section 4: Support and Resources**

11. How available and helpful were the course instructors and support staff?

12. Were the course materials and resources (e.g., textbooks, online resources) adequate and relevant?

13. Were there any technical issues or difficulties that hindered your learning experience?

**Section 5: Additional Comments**

14. Do you have any additional comments or suggestions about the course?

15. Is there anything we could have done differently to improve your learning experience?

**Section 6: Demographics**

16. What is your role/position in the company?

17. How long have you been working for the company?

18. What is your current level of education (e.g., Bachelor's, Master's, Doctorate)?

19. How would you rate your overall level of satisfaction with the company's training and development programs?

Thank you for taking the time to provide your feedback! Your input is invaluable in helping us improve our courses and training programs.

Please note that this is just a sample questionnaire, and you can modify it to fit your specific needs and requirements.

c) Neutral
d) Somewhat Dissatisfied
e) Very Dissatisfied

b) Occasionally

c) Depends on the situation

[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a sample questionnaire on Access to Technology and Tools:

**Access to Technology and Tools Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
As part of our ongoing efforts to improve the work environment and employee satisfaction, we would like to gather your thoughts and opinions on access to technology and tools within the company. Your responses will help us understand the current state of technology access and identify areas for improvement.

**Section 1: Current Technology Access**

1. How often do you use company-provided technology (e.g., computers, software, mobile devices) for work purposes?

a) Daily
b) Several times a week
c) Occasionally
d) Rarely

2. What types of technology do you typically use for work? (Check all that apply)

a) Computers
b) Mobile devices (smartphones, tablets)
c) Software (e.g., Microsoft Office, specialized tools)
d) Other (please specify)

3. How satisfied are you with the current technology infrastructure and tools provided by the company?

a) Very satisfied
b) Somewhat satisfied
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat dissatisfied
e) Very dissatisfied

4. Have you experienced any issues or challenges when trying to access company technology or tools? If yes, please describe.

**Section 2: Barriers to Access**

1. What do you think is the biggest barrier to accessing technology and tools within the company? (Check all that apply)

a) Lack of training or support
b) Technical issues or maintenance downtime
c) Limited availability or accessibility
d) Company policies or security restrictions
e) Other (please specify)

2. Have you ever encountered any technical issues or problems when trying to access technology or tools? If yes, how did you resolve them?

**Section 3: Future Needs and Preferences**

1. What new technology or tools would you like to have access to in the future? (Check all that apply)

[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a sample questionnaire on Career Path Clarity:

**Career Path Clarity Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
Thank you for participating in this survey! We're interested in understanding your thoughts and experiences regarding career path clarity within our organization. Your responses will help us identify areas for improvement and create a more supportive environment for your professional growth.

**Section 1: Career Goals and Aspirations**

1. What are your top three career goals for the next 12-18 months?

a) _______________________________________________________
b) _______________________________________________________
c) _______________________________________________________

2. How important is it for you to have a clear understanding of your career path within the company? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "Not important at all" and 5 is "Very important")

3. Have you ever felt uncertain or unclear about your career path within the company? If yes, please describe the situation and how it made you feel.

**Section 2: Career Development and Support**

1. How satisfied are you with the career development opportunities available to you within the company? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "Very dissatisfied" and 5 is "Very satisfied")

2. Have you received any formal or informal feedback on your performance or career development from your supervisor or mentor? If yes, please describe the feedback and its impact on your career path.

3. How important is it for you to have a mentor or coach who can guide and support your career development? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "Not important at all" and 5 is "Very important")

**Section 3: Communication and Transparency**

1. How would you rate the transparency of communication regarding company goals, objectives, and expectations? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "Not transparent at all" and 5 is "Very transparent")

2. Have you ever felt confused or unclear about company expectations or priorities? If yes, please describe the situation and how it affected your work.

3. How often do you receive regular updates or progress reports on company initiatives and goals? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "Rarely" and 5 is "Frequently")

**Section 4: Career Path Clarity and Job Satisfaction**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how clear are you about your career path and opportunities for growth within the company? (1 = Not clear at all, 5 = Very clear)

2. How satisfied are you with your current job and role within the company? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "Very dissatisfied" and 5 is "Very satisfied")

3. Have you ever considered leaving the company due to unclear career prospects or lack of opportunities for growth? If yes, please describe the situation and why you considered leaving.

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to share your thoughts and experiences with us! Your input is invaluable in helping us create a more supportive environment for your career growth and development.

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a sample questionnaire on Career Path Clarity:

**Career Path Clarity Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
We're interested in understanding how well you understand your career path and opportunities for growth within our organization. Your responses will help us identify areas where we can improve and provide more clarity for you and your colleagues.

**Section 1: Current Career Situation**

1. What is your current job title and department?
2. How satisfied are you with your current job and career path? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "not satisfied at all" and 5 is "very satisfied")
3. What are your greatest strengths and accomplishments in your current role?

**Section 2: Career Goals and Aspirations**

1. What are your short-term career goals (next 1-2 years)? Please be specific.
2. What are your long-term career goals (next 5-10 years)? Please be specific.
3. What motivates you to achieve your career goals?

**Section 3: Career Development and Support**

1. Have you received any formal training or mentorship to support your career development? If so, what was it and how has it helped?
2. Do you feel like you have a clear understanding of the skills and qualifications needed for your desired career path? If not, what would help you gain a better understanding?
3. How important is career development and growth to you? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "not important at all" and 5 is "very important")

**Section 4: Barriers to Career Advancement**

1. What, if anything, do you feel is holding you back from advancing in your career? (Select all that apply)
	* Lack of opportunities
	* Limited resources or budget
	* Limited visibility or recognition
	* Other (please specify)
2. Have you experienced any biases or discrimination that have impacted your career advancement? If so, please describe.
3. Are there any specific skills or knowledge gaps that you feel you need to address to advance in your career?

**Section 5: Company Support and Resources**

1. How satisfied are you with the company's support and resources for career development? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "not satisfied at all" and 5 is "very satisfied")
2. Have you taken advantage of any company-sponsored training or development programs? If so, what was it and how has it helped?
3. Are there any specific company resources or programs that you feel are missing or could be improved to support career development?

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to provide your feedback on career path clarity. Your input will help us better understand the needs and concerns of our employees and identify areas for improvement.

Feel free to modify or add questions as needed to fit your specific goals and objectives!

**Employee Motivation Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
We're interested in understanding what drives and motivates our employees to excel in their roles and contribute to the company's success. Your input will help us identify areas for improvement and develop strategies to boost morale and productivity.

**Section 1: Job Satisfaction**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how satisfied are you with your current job role?

(Scale: 1 = Very dissatisfied, 2 = Somewhat dissatisfied, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat satisfied, 5 = Very satisfied)

2. What aspects of your job do you enjoy the most? (Select all that apply)

* Sense of accomplishment
* Opportunities for growth and development
* Collaboration with colleagues
* Autonomy and independence
* Other (please specify)

3. Are there any aspects of your job that you find unfulfilling or demotivating? If yes, please describe.

**Section 2: Recognition and Rewards**

4. How often do you receive recognition or feedback for your work from your supervisor or colleagues?

* Daily
* Weekly
* Monthly
* Rarely
* Never

5. What types of recognition or rewards would motivate you to perform better? (Select all that apply)

* Public recognition
* Monetary rewards
* Additional time off
* Professional development opportunities
* Other (please specify)

6. Have you ever received an unexpected reward or recognition for your work? If yes, how did it make you feel?

**Section 3: Work-Life Balance**

7. How would you rate your current work-life balance?

(Scale: 1 = Poor, 2 = Fair, 3 = Good, 4 = Excellent, 5 = Outstanding)

8. What steps can we take to improve work-life balance for you? (Select all that apply)

* Flexible scheduling
* Telecommuting options
* Employee wellness programs
* Professional development opportunities
* Other (please specify)

**Section 4: Communication and Feedback**

9. How would you rate the quality of communication from your supervisor or manager?

(Scale: 1 = Poor, 2 = Fair, 3 = Good, 4 = Excellent, 5 = Outstanding)

10. Do you feel like your opinions and ideas are valued and considered in decision-making processes? If not, what changes would you suggest?

**Section 5: Overall Motivation**

11. On a scale of 1-5, how motivated are you to come to work and contribute to the company's success?

(Scale: 1 = Not motivated at all, 2 = Somewhat motivated, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat motivated, 5 = Highly motivated)

12. What would make you feel more motivated and engaged at work? (Open-ended question)

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to share your thoughts and opinions on employee motivation. Your input is invaluable in helping us create a more motivated and productive workforce.

**Section 1: Job Satisfaction**

(Yes/No)

2. If not, what obstacles have you faced in achieving your goals?

3. What do you think would help you achieve your goals more effectively?

(Scale: 1-5)

2. Do you feel you receive regular and constructive feedback on your performance?

(Yes/No)

3. What types of feedback would you like to receive more often?

(Yes/No)

2. Are there any job responsibilities that you feel are unnecessary or not aligned with your role?

(Yes/No)

3. What changes would you suggest to make your job more engaging and challenging?

(Yes/No)

(1 = Very Dissatisfied, 2 = Somewhat Dissatisfied, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Satisfied, 5 = Very Satisfied)

Here's a questionnaire on Feedback Mechanisms:

**Feedback Mechanisms Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
We value your input and would like to understand your experiences with our current feedback mechanisms. Your responses will help us improve our processes and better serve our employees.

**Section 1: Current Feedback Mechanisms**

1. How often do you provide feedback to your supervisor or HR department?

a) Daily
b) Weekly
c) Monthly
d) Quarterly
e) Rarely

2. What feedback mechanisms do you currently use to share your thoughts and suggestions? (Select all that apply)

a) Regular meetings with supervisor
b) Email or online forms
c) Surveys or online polls
d) In-person meetings or focus groups
e) Other (please specify)

3. How effective do you think our current feedback mechanisms are in addressing your concerns and suggestions?

a) Very effective
b) Somewhat effective
c) Not very effective
d) Not at all effective

**Section 2: Feedback Mechanisms Satisfaction**

1. How satisfied are you with the current feedback mechanisms?

a) Very satisfied
b) Somewhat satisfied
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat dissatisfied
e) Very dissatisfied

2. What do you think is the most important aspect of a feedback mechanism?

a) Timeliness of response
b) Transparency of process
c) Opportunity for anonymous feedback
d) Frequency of feedback
e) Other (please specify)

	* Weekly
	* Monthly
	* Quarterly
	* Rarely

	* Positive feedback
	* Constructive feedback
	* Suggestions for improvement
	* Recognition for a job well done
	* Other (please specify)

	* I usually take it seriously, but sometimes I don't agree
	* I rarely take it seriously
	* I don't receive feedback from others

	* Regular check-ins with managers or mentors
	* Anonymous feedback systems
	* Peer-to-peer feedback mechanisms
	* Performance reviews with clear goals and expectations
	* Other (please specify)
2. Would you prefer to receive feedback in a:
	* Formal setting (e.g. performance review)
	* Informal setting (e.g. casual conversation)
	* Written format (e.g. email or report)
	* Other (please specify)
3. How important is it to you that feedback is:
	* Timely (i.e. received in a timely manner)
	* Actionable (i.e. provides clear steps for improvement)
	* Constructive (i.e. focuses on specific behaviors or actions)
	* Other (please specify)

2. Is there anything you'd like to see changed or improved about our current feedback mechanisms?

d) Other (please specify)

Here is a sample questionnaire on Health and Safety Measures:

**Health and Safety Measures Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
As part of our ongoing efforts to ensure a safe and healthy work environment, we would like to gather your thoughts and opinions on our current health and safety measures. Your input will help us identify areas for improvement and implement changes to better protect our employees.

**Section 1: Awareness and Training**

1. How often do you receive training on health and safety procedures?
a) Daily
b) Weekly
c) Monthly
d) Quarterly
e) Rarely

2. Have you received training on emergency procedures (e.g., fire evacuation, first aid)?
a) Yes
b) No

3. Do you feel confident in your ability to respond to a health and safety emergency?
a) Yes
b) No

4. What do you think is the most effective way to improve health and safety training in our organization?

**Section 2: Workplace Conditions**

1. How would you rate the overall cleanliness and organization of your workspace?
a) Excellent
b) Good
c) Fair
d) Poor

2. Are there any areas in your workspace that you feel are hazardous or potentially hazardous?
(Open-ended question)

3. Do you have access to necessary personal protective equipment (PPE) and tools?
a) Yes
b) No

4. Are there any areas in your workspace where you feel exposed to noise, chemicals, or other hazards?
(Open-ended question)

**Section 3: Reporting Incidents**

1. How often do you report near-miss incidents or minor accidents to your supervisor or HR?
a) Always
b) Sometimes
c) Rarely
d) Never

2. Have you ever experienced a serious injury or illness while on the job?
a) Yes
b) No

3. Do you feel comfortable reporting incidents or concerns without fear of retribution?
a) Yes
b) No

4. What would you like to see changed or improved in our reporting process?

**Section 4: General Feedback**

1. What do you think is the most important health and safety measure that we could implement to improve our workplace?

2. Are there any specific health and safety concerns or issues that you would like to see addressed?

3. Do you have any suggestions for improving our overall health and safety culture?

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to complete this questionnaire. Your input is invaluable in helping us create a safer and healthier work environment. If you have any additional comments or suggestions, please feel free to include them below.

I hope this helps! Let me know if you need any further assistance.

**Health and Safety Measures Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
The purpose of this questionnaire is to gather information about your experiences and perceptions regarding health and safety measures within our organization. Your responses will help us identify areas for improvement and develop effective strategies to ensure a safe and healthy work environment.

**Section 1: General Perceptions**

1. How would you rate your overall satisfaction with the health and safety measures in place within our organization?

(Scale: 1 = Very Dissatisfied, 2 = Somewhat Dissatisfied, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Satisfied, 5 = Very Satisfied)

2. Have you ever experienced a near-miss or close call while working? If yes, please describe the incident.

3. Do you feel that your supervisor or manager is committed to health and safety in the workplace? Why or why not?

**Section 2: Training and Awareness**

1. Have you received any formal training on health and safety procedures? If yes, what type of training?

2. How would you rate the effectiveness of our health and safety training programs?

(Scale: 1 = Not Effective, 2 = Somewhat Effective, 3 = Very Effective, 4 = Extremely Effective)

3. Are you aware of the emergency procedures in place (e.g., evacuation routes, first aid kits)? If yes, how confident do you feel in your ability to follow these procedures?

**Section 3: Work Environment**

1. Do you feel that your workspace is clean and well-maintained? Why or why not?

2. Are there any areas of concern regarding hazardous materials or equipment in your work area?

3. Do you experience any physical or mental discomfort while working (e.g., eye strain, back pain)? If yes, please describe.

**Section 4: Reporting Incidents**

1. Have you ever reported a health and safety incident or concern to your supervisor or HR department? If yes, what was the outcome?

2. Do you feel comfortable reporting incidents or concerns without fear of retribution or negative consequences?

3. Are there any barriers or challenges you face when reporting incidents or concerns?

**Section 5: Suggestions and Comments**

1. What do you think is the most important health and safety measure that we could implement or improve?

2. Do you have any suggestions for improving our health and safety procedures or training programs?

3. Is there anything else you would like to share about health and safety in our organization?

Thank you for taking the time to complete this questionnaire. Your input is invaluable in helping us prioritize health and safety initiatives.

**Internal Mobility Opportunities Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
As part of our ongoing efforts to support employee growth and development, we're interested in understanding your experiences and opinions on internal mobility opportunities within the company. Your feedback will help us identify areas for improvement and create more opportunities for employees to advance their careers.

**Section 1: Current Job Satisfaction**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how satisfied are you with your current job?

(Scale: 1 = Very dissatisfied, 2 = Somewhat dissatisfied, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat satisfied, 5 = Very satisfied)

2. What aspects of your current job do you enjoy the most? (Select all that apply)

* Challenging work
* Opportunities for growth and development
* Collaborative work environment
* Autonomy and independence
* Other (please specify)

**Section 2: Internal Mobility Experiences**

1. Have you ever taken advantage of an internal mobility opportunity (e.g., job rotation, transfer, promotion) within the company?

Yes No

2. If yes, what motivated you to pursue internal mobility? (Select all that apply)

* Desire for new challenges
* Career advancement opportunities
* Desire for a change of pace or work environment
* Other (please specify)

3. If yes, what was your experience like? (Scale: 1-5)

* Extremely positive
* Somewhat positive
* Neutral
* Somewhat negative
* Extremely negative

**Section 3: Barriers to Internal Mobility**

1. What barriers, if any, have you faced in pursuing internal mobility opportunities? (Select all that apply)

* Lack of awareness about available opportunities
* Limited job openings or competition for positions
* Fear of leaving a comfortable role or familiar work environment
* Concerns about impact on current team or colleagues
* Other (please specify)

2. How important is it for you to have internal mobility opportunities available within the company? (Scale: 1-5)

* Very important
* Somewhat important
* Neutral
* Somewhat unimportant
* Very unimportant

**Section 4: Suggestions for Improvement**

1. What would you like to see changed or improved about internal mobility opportunities within the company? (Open-ended question)

2. Are there any specific internal mobility opportunities or programs that you would like to see implemented? (Open-ended question)

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to share your thoughts and experiences on internal mobility opportunities within the company. Your feedback is invaluable in helping us create a more dynamic and supportive work environment.

**Introduction:** Thank you for participating in our recent kick-off meeting! Your feedback is invaluable in helping us improve our team's collaboration and project execution. Please take a few minutes to share your thoughts on the meeting's effectiveness and suggestions for future improvements.

**Section 1: Overall Satisfaction**

**Section 2: Meeting Content and Structure**

1. Were the meeting's objectives and agenda clearly communicated beforehand?

(Scale: 1 = Strongly disagree, 2 = Somewhat disagree, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat agree, 5 = Strongly agree)

2. Were the topics and discussions relevant and engaging?

(Scale: 1 = Strongly disagree, 2 = Somewhat disagree, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat agree, 5 = Strongly agree)

3. Were there any topics or areas that you felt were missing or under-discussed?

(Open-ended text field for respondents to share their thoughts)

(Scale: 1 = Strongly disagree, 2 = Somewhat disagree, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat agree, 5 = Strongly agree)

2. Were there any moments of tension or conflict during the meeting?

(Scale: 1 = Yes, significant; 2 = Yes, minor; 3 = No)

3. How would you rate the overall team spirit and morale during the meeting?

(Scale: 1 = Very low, 2 = Low, 3 = Neutral, 4 = High, 5 = Very high)

**Section 4: Suggestions for Improvement**

1. What changes or adjustments would you suggest to improve the kick-off meeting's effectiveness?

(Open-ended text field for respondents to share their thoughts)

(Open-ended text field for respondents to share their thoughts)

Here is a sample questionnaire on Leadership Effectiveness:

**Leadership Effectiveness Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
The purpose of this questionnaire is to gather feedback on the leadership effectiveness of our managers. Your responses will help us understand what our leaders do well and where they can improve. Please answer the questions honestly and to the best of your ability.

**Section 1: Overall Leadership**

1. How would you rate the overall leadership of your manager?

a) Excellent
b) Good
c) Fair
d) Poor

2. What are your manager's greatest strengths as a leader?

(Open-ended question)

3. What are your manager's areas for improvement as a leader?

(Open-ended question)

**Section 2: Communication**

4. How would you rate your manager's communication style?

a) Clear and concise
b) Sometimes clear, sometimes unclear
c) Unclear or confusing
d) Non-existent

5. Do you feel like your manager listens to your concerns and ideas?

a) Always
b) Most of the time
c) Sometimes
d) Rarely

6. How would you rate your manager's ability to provide feedback and constructive criticism?

a) Excellent
b) Good
c) Fair
d) Poor

**Section 3: Decision-Making**

7. How would you rate your manager's decision-making process?

a) Well-thought-out and transparent
b) Reasonable, but sometimes unclear
c) Impulsive or unexplained
d) Non-existent

8. Do you feel like your manager involves you in decision-making processes?

a) Always
b) Most of the time
c) Sometimes
d) Rarely

9. How would you rate your manager's willingness to take calculated risks?

a) Excellent
b) Good
c) Fair
d) Poor

**Section 4: Emotional Intelligence**

10. How would you rate your manager's emotional intelligence (ability to understand and manage their own emotions and those of others)?

a) Excellent
b) Good
c) Fair
d) Poor

11. Do you feel like your manager is empathetic and understanding?

a) Always
b) Most of the time
c) Sometimes
d) Rarely

12. How would you rate your manager's ability to manage conflict and difficult situations?

a) Excellent
b) Good
c) Fair
d) Poor

**Section 5: Empowerment**

13. Do you feel like your manager gives you the autonomy to make decisions and take ownership of your work?

a) Always
b) Most of the time
c) Sometimes
d) Rarely

14. How would you rate your manager's ability to empower others to take on new responsibilities?

a) Excellent
b) Good
c) Fair
d) Poor

15. Do you feel like your manager provides the necessary resources and support to help you succeed?

a) Always
b) Most of the time
c) Sometimes
d) Rarely

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to provide your feedback on your manager's leadership effectiveness. Your input is invaluable in helping us improve our leadership development programs and support our managers in becoming more effective leaders.

Please note that this is just a sample questionnaire, and you may want to modify it to fit your specific needs and goals.

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a questionnaire on Leadership Effectiveness:

**Leadership Effectiveness Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
As part of our ongoing efforts to improve leadership development, we would like to gather your insights on the effectiveness of our leaders. Your input will help us identify areas of strength and weakness, and inform our strategies for future growth and development.

**Section 1: Leadership Style**

1. How would you describe your supervisor's leadership style? (Scale: 1 = Autocratic, 2 = Democratic, 3 = Transformational)
2. Do you feel your supervisor is approachable and open to feedback? (Scale: 1 = Strongly Disagree, 2 = Somewhat Disagree, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Agree, 5 = Strongly Agree)
3. How often does your supervisor provide clear goals and expectations? (Scale: 1 = Rarely, 2 = Occasionally, 3 = Frequently, 4 = Almost Always, 5 = Always)

**Section 2: Communication**

4. How would you rate the quality of communication from your supervisor? (Scale: 1 = Poor, 2 = Fair, 3 = Good, 4 = Excellent)
5. Do you feel your supervisor actively listens to your concerns and ideas? (Scale: 1 = Strongly Disagree, 2 = Somewhat Disagree, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Agree, 5 = Strongly Agree)
6. How often do you receive regular updates on the team's progress and goals? (Scale: 1 = Rarely, 2 = Occasionally, 3 = Frequently, 4 = Almost Always, 5 = Always)

**Section 3: Decision-Making**

7. How would you rate the speed and decisiveness of your supervisor's decision-making? (Scale: 1 = Slow, 2 = Average, 3 = Quick)
8. Do you feel your supervisor involves you in decision-making processes? (Scale: 1 = Strongly Disagree, 2 = Somewhat Disagree, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Agree, 5 = Strongly Agree)
9. How often do you see your supervisor taking calculated risks to drive innovation and growth? (Scale: 1 = Rarely, 2 = Occasionally, 3 = Frequently, 4 = Almost Always, 5 = Always)

**Section 4: Employee Engagement**

10. How would you rate your overall job satisfaction? (Scale: 1 = Very Dissatisfied, 2 = Somewhat Dissatisfied, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Satisfied, 5 = Very Satisfied)
11. Do you feel motivated and inspired by your supervisor's leadership? (Scale: 1 = Strongly Disagree, 2 = Somewhat Disagree, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Agree, 5 = Strongly Agree)
12. How often do you feel recognized and rewarded for your contributions? (Scale: 1 = Rarely, 2 = Occasionally, 3 = Frequently, 4 = Almost Always, 5 = Always)

**Section 5: Additional Comments**

13. Is there anything your supervisor does exceptionally well that you'd like to see more of?
14. Are there any areas where you feel your supervisor could improve or provide more support?

**Thank you for taking the time to provide your valuable feedback! Your input will help us create a more effective and supportive leadership culture.**

Let me know if you'd like me to convert this questionnaire into a specific format (e.g. Excel, Word, PDF).

**Section 1: Pre-Onboarding**

1. How did you first learn about the company and the job opening that led to your employment?

a) Job posting on our website
b) Social media
c) Referral from a current employee or friend
d) Recruitment agency
e) Other (please specify)

2. What was your impression of the company culture and values before joining?

a) Very positive
b) Somewhat positive
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat negative
e) Very negative

3. Were you provided with any pre-onboarding materials (e.g. company literature, video, etc.)?

a) Yes
b) No

**Section 2: Onboarding Process**

4. How would you rate the overall onboarding experience?

a) Excellent
b) Good
c) Fair
d) Poor

5. Which of the following best describes your experience during the onboarding process?

a) Well-organized and structured
b) Somewhat organized, but with some confusion
c) Unorganized and confusing
d) Other (please specify)

6. What did you find most helpful during the onboarding process?

a) Meeting with HR or a designated onboarding representative
b) Orientation sessions
c) Training or workshops
d) Mentorship or buddy system
e) Other (please specify)

7. What did you find most challenging during the onboarding process?

a) Learning new systems and processes
b) Meeting new people and building relationships
c) Understanding company policies and procedures
d) Other (please specify)

**Section 3: Post-Onboarding**

8. How would you rate your overall satisfaction with the onboarding experience?

a) Very satisfied
b) Somewhat satisfied
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat dissatisfied
e) Very dissatisfied

9. Have you felt prepared to start your new role after the onboarding process?

a) Yes
b) No

**Onboarding Experience Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
The purpose of this questionnaire is to understand your onboarding experience at [Company Name]. Your feedback will help us identify areas of improvement and make necessary changes to enhance the onboarding process. Please answer the questions honestly, and we appreciate your time in providing this valuable feedback.

**Section 1: Pre-Onboarding Experience**

1. How did you learn about the onboarding process before your first day at [Company Name]? (Select all that apply)
	* HR communication
	* Manager communication
	* Online resources (e.g., company website, intranet)
	* Colleagues' recommendations
	* Other (please specify)
2. Did you feel prepared for your first day at [Company Name]?
	* Yes
	* No
	* Neutral
3. What were your expectations about the onboarding process before your first day?

**Section 2: Onboarding Experience**

1. How would you rate the overall onboarding experience at [Company Name]?
	* Excellent
	* Good
	* Fair
	* Poor
2. What were the most helpful aspects of the onboarding process? (Select all that apply)
	* Orientation sessions
	* Meeting with HR or manager
	* Access to company resources (e.g., intranet, documentation)
	* Networking with colleagues
	* Other (please specify)
3. What were the most challenging aspects of the onboarding process? (Select all that apply)
	* Lack of clear instructions
	* Limited access to information
	* Difficulty in finding the right people to ask questions
	* Feeling overwhelmed
	* Other (please specify)
4. Did you receive any feedback or evaluations during the onboarding process?
	* Yes
	* No
	* Partially (please specify)

**Section 3: Post-Onboarding Experience**

1. How long did it take you to feel comfortable in your new role?
	* Less than a week
	* 1-2 weeks
	* 2-4 weeks
	* More than 4 weeks
2. Have you experienced any difficulties or challenges since the onboarding process? If so, please describe.
3. Have you received any recognition or rewards for your performance since the onboarding process?
	* Yes
	* No
	* Partially (please specify)

**Section 4: Additional Comments**

1. Do you have any suggestions or ideas for improving the onboarding process at [Company Name]?
2. Is there anything you would like to highlight or emphasize about your onboarding experience?

**Thank you for taking the time to provide your feedback! Your input is invaluable in helping us improve the onboarding process at [Company Name].**

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a sample questionnaire on Onboarding Experience:

**Onboarding Experience Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
We're interested in understanding your experience during the onboarding process at our company. Your feedback will help us improve our onboarding process and ensure that new hires have a seamless transition into their new roles.

**Section 1: Pre-Onboarding Experience**

1. How did you learn about our company's onboarding process before your first day? (Select all that apply)
	* Through HR communication
	* Through a colleague or supervisor
	* Online research
	* Other (please specify)
2. Were you provided with any pre-onboarding materials (e.g., employee handbook, company policies, etc.)? If yes, how helpful were they?
3. Did you feel prepared for your first day at the company? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "not at all" and 5 is "very")

**Section 2: Onboarding Process**

1. What was your overall impression of the onboarding process? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "poor" and 5 is "excellent")
2. How would you rate the clarity of the onboarding process? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "not clear at all" and 5 is "very clear")
3. Were there any specific onboarding activities or training sessions that you found particularly helpful or unhelpful? If yes, please describe.
4. Did you feel supported by your supervisor or HR during the onboarding process? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "not at all" and 5 is "very")

**Section 3: Onboarding Outcomes**

1. How would you rate the effectiveness of the onboarding process in helping you understand your role and responsibilities? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "not effective at all" and 5 is "very effective")
2. Have you experienced any challenges or difficulties during the onboarding process? If yes, please describe.
3. Have you felt a sense of belonging or connection to the company culture during the onboarding process? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "not at all" and 5 is "very")

**Section 4: Additional Comments**

1. Do you have any suggestions for improving the onboarding process?
2. Is there anything that you wish you had known before starting your onboarding process?
3. Any additional comments or feedback about your onboarding experience?

Thank you for taking the time to provide your feedback! Your input is invaluable in helping us improve our onboarding process.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Onboarding Experience

2. Were you provided with any pre-onboarding materials (e.g., employee handbook, company policies, etc.)? If yes, how helpful were they?

1. What was your overall impression of the onboarding process? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "poor" and 5 is "excellent")
2. How would you rate the clarity of the onboarding process? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "not clear at all" and 5 is "very clear")
3. Were there any specific onboarding activities or training sessions that you found particularly helpful or unhelpful? If yes, please describe.
4. Did you feel supported by your supervisor or HR during the onboarding process? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "not at all" and 5 is "very")

**Section 3: Onboarding Outcomes**

1. How would you rate the effectiveness of the onboarding process in helping you understand your role and responsibilities? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "not effective at all" and 5 is "very effective")
2. Have you experienced any challenges or difficulties during the onboarding process? If yes, please describe.
3. Have you felt a sense of belonging or connection to the company culture during the onboarding process? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "not at all" and 5 is "very")

2. Is there anything that you wish you had known before starting your onboarding process?

c) Monthly
d) Rarely

d) Non-monetary rewards (e.g., extra time off, flexible scheduling)
e) Other (please specify)

a) Very important
b) Somewhat important
c) Not very important
d) Not at all important

a) Public recognition
b) Private recognition
c) Monetary rewards

e) Other (please specify)

a) Specific achievements (e.g., meeting targets, completing projects)

c) Innovation and creativity
d) Teamwork and collaboration
e) Other (please specify)

a) In-person (e.g., during a meeting or celebration)

c) Through a dedicated recognition platform (e.g., employee recognition app)
d) Other (please specify)

**Section 3: Barriers to Recognition and Rewards**

a) Lack of clear expectations or criteria for recognition
b) Limited opportunities for recognition
c) Competition with colleagues for recognition
d) Other (please specify)

a) Yes
b) Somewhat
c) Not very
d) Not at all

**Introduction:** We value our employees' hard work and dedication. To better understand what motivates and inspires you, we'd like to hear your thoughts on recognition and rewards. Your feedback will help us create a more rewarding and engaging work environment.

**Section 1: Recognition**

1. How often do you feel recognized for your achievements at work?

a) Frequently (e.g., weekly/monthly)
b) Occasionally (e.g., quarterly/yearly)
c) Rarely
d) Never

2. What forms of recognition do you value most? (Select up to 3)

a) Public recognition (e.g., company-wide announcements)
b) Private recognition (e.g., one-on-one feedback)
c) Monetary rewards (e.g., bonuses, gift cards)
d) Non-monetary rewards (e.g., extra time off, flexible work arrangements)
e) Other (please specify)

3. Have you ever received a surprise recognition or reward? If so, how did it make you feel?

4. What do you think is the most effective way for your manager to recognize your contributions?

**Section 2: Rewards**

1. What motivates you to go above and beyond at work? (Select up to 2)

a) Financial rewards
b) Recognition and praise
c) Career advancement opportunities
d) Work-life balance
e) Other (please specify)

2. Would you prefer a one-time reward or a series of smaller rewards?

a) One-time reward
b) Series of smaller rewards
c) Either is fine

3. What type of rewards do you think would be most effective in motivating you? (Select up to 2)

a) Monetary rewards (e.g., bonuses, gift cards)
b) Non-monetary rewards (e.g., extra time off, flexible work arrangements)
c) Professional development opportunities (e.g., training, mentorship)
d) Other (please specify)

4. Have you ever received a reward that didn't quite align with your values or interests? If so, how did you feel?

**Section 3: Open-Ended Questions**

1. What do you think is the most important aspect of recognition and rewards in the workplace?

2. Can you think of a time when you felt undervalued or underappreciated? What happened, and how did you feel?

3. Are there any recognition or reward programs that you think would be beneficial to the company or your team? If so, please describe.

**Conclusion:** Thank you for taking the time to share your thoughts on recognition and rewards. Your feedback is invaluable in helping us create a more rewarding and engaging work environment.

Please note that this is just a sample questionnaire, and you can modify it according to your specific needs and goals.

**Smart Working Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
As part of our ongoing efforts to improve work-life balance and employee satisfaction, we're conducting a survey to understand your experiences and opinions on Smart Working. Your responses will help us shape our policies and practices to better support your needs.

**Section 1: Current Work Arrangements**

1. What is your current work arrangement (check all that apply)?

* Traditional office-based
* Hybrid (mix of office and remote work)
* Fully remote
* Flexible hours (e.g., flexible start/end times, compressed workweeks)
* Other (please specify)

2. How often do you work from home or remotely?

* Daily
* Several times a week
* Occasionally
* Rarely
* Never

3. What are the most common reasons you work from home or remotely (check all that apply)?

* To take care of personal matters (e.g., family, health)
* To reduce commuting time and stress
* To improve work-life balance
* To increase productivity and focus
* Other (please specify)

**Section 2: Smart Working Preferences**

1. Which of the following Smart Working arrangements would you prefer (check all that apply)?

* Flexible hours
* Flexible days off
* Telecommuting (full-time or part-time)
* Compressed workweeks
* Job sharing
* Other (please specify)

2. How important is it for you to have a dedicated workspace at home for work purposes?

* Very important
* Somewhat important
* Not very important
* Not at all important

3. Would you prefer to have more autonomy in determining your own work schedule?

* Yes
* No
* Undecided

**Section 3: Challenges and Opportunities**

1. What are the biggest challenges you face when working remotely or in a Smart Working arrangement (check all that apply)?

* Difficulty separating work and personal life
* Limited access to company resources or support
* Difficulty staying connected with colleagues and management
* Feeling isolated or disconnected
* Other (please specify)

2. What are the most significant benefits you've experienced from Smart Working (check all that apply)?

* Improved work-life balance
* Increased productivity and focus
* Reduced commuting time and stress
* Better overall well-being
* Other (please specify)

**Section 4: Additional Comments**

1. Do you have any suggestions or ideas for improving our Smart Working policies and practices?

2. Are there any specific tools, technologies, or resources you think would enhance your Smart Working experience?

**Conclusion:**
Thank you for taking the time to participate in this survey! Your input is invaluable in helping us shape our Smart Working policies and practices. If you have any questions or concerns, please don't hesitate to reach out to us.

Let me know if you need any modifications or if you'd like me to convert this into a specific format (e.g., Google Forms, Excel, Word).

	* Technical skills
	* Soft skills (e.g., communication, teamwork, time management)
	* Leadership and management
	* Industry-specific knowledge
	* Other (please specify): _______________________________________________________
4. How do you prefer to learn new skills or information? (Select all that apply)
	* Classroom-style training
	* Online courses or webinars
	* On-the-job training or mentoring
	* Workshops or seminars
	* Self-paced learning (e.g., books, articles, online tutorials)
	* Other (please specify): _______________________________________________________
5. Are there any specific training or development programs you have not had the opportunity to participate in, but would like to? If so, please specify: _______________________________________________________

**Section 3: Training Evaluation**

6. How would you rate the relevance of the training to your current job responsibilities? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "not relevant" and 5 is "very relevant")
7. How would you rate the effectiveness of the training in improving your skills or knowledge? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "not effective" and 5 is "very effective")
8. Have you applied any of the skills or knowledge learned from training to your work? If so, please describe: _______________________________________________________
9. Would you recommend the training program to your colleagues? (Yes/No)
	* If yes, please specify why: _______________________________________________________
	* If no, please specify why: _______________________________________________________

**Section 4: Additional Comments and Suggestions**

10. Do you have any additional comments or suggestions about our training and development programs? _______________________________________________________
11. Is there anything we could do to improve the training experience for you and your colleagues? _______________________________________________________

**Training and Development Programs Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
Thank you for participating in this survey! Your feedback is crucial in helping us understand the effectiveness of our training and development programs. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to provide any additional comments or suggestions.

**Section 1: Current Training Experience**

1. Have you participated in any training programs or workshops within the past 6 months? (Yes/No)
	* If yes, please specify the type of training (e.g., technical, soft skills, leadership, etc.): _______________________________________________________
2. How would you rate the overall quality of the training you received? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "not satisfactory" and 5 is "excellent")

**Section 2: Training Needs and Preferences**

3. Which of the following topics would you like to see more training on? (Select all that apply)
	* Technical skills
	* Soft skills (e.g., communication, teamwork, time management)
	* Leadership and management
	* Industry-specific knowledge
	* Other (please specify): _______________________________________________________
4. How do you prefer to learn new skills or information? (Select all that apply)
	* Classroom-style training
	* Online courses or webinars
	* On-the-job training or mentoring
	* Workshops or seminars
	* Self-paced learning (e.g., books, articles, online tutorials)
	* Other (please specify): _______________________________________________________
5. Are there any specific training or development programs you have not had the opportunity to participate in, but would like to? If so, please specify: _______________________________________________________

**Section 3: Training Evaluation**

6. How would you rate the relevance of the training to your current job responsibilities? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "not relevant" and 5 is "very relevant")
7. How would you rate the effectiveness of the training in improving your skills or knowledge? (Scale: 1-5, where 1 is "not effective" and 5 is "very effective")
8. Have you applied any of the skills or knowledge learned from training to your work? If so, please describe: _______________________________________________________
9. Would you recommend the training program to your colleagues? (Yes/No)
	* If yes, please specify why: _______________________________________________________
	* If no, please specify why: _______________________________________________________

**Section 4: Additional Comments and Suggestions**

10. Do you have any additional comments or suggestions about our training and development programs? _______________________________________________________
11. Is there anything we could do to improve the training experience for you and your colleagues? _______________________________________________________

Thank you for taking the time to participate in this survey! Your feedback is invaluable in helping us create a more effective and engaging training and development program.

**Training and Development Programs Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
We are interested in understanding your experiences and perceptions about the training and development programs offered by our organization. 	* Technical skills (e.g., software, tools, methodologies)
	* Leadership and management
	* Communication and interpersonal skills
	* Time management and productivity
	* Industry trends and best practices
	* Other (please specify)

	* Frequently (every few months)
	* Occasionally (every 6-12 months)
	* Rarely (less than once a year)
	* Never

3. What motivates you to participate in training and development programs? (Select all that apply)
	* Career advancement opportunities
	* Personal growth and learning
	* Improved job performance and efficiency
	* Networking and collaboration opportunities
	* Recognition and rewards
	* Other (please specify)

	* (List specific programs, e.g., leadership development, technical training, etc.)

	* Excellent
	* Good
	* Fair
	* Poor
	* Not applicable

6. What do you think is the most valuable aspect of our training and development programs? (Select one)
	* Practical application and hands-on learning
	* Networking and collaboration opportunities
	* Access to industry experts and thought leaders
	* Opportunities for career advancement and growth
	* Other (please specify)

**Training and Development Programs Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
Thank you for participating in this survey! Your feedback is crucial in helping us understand the effectiveness of our training and development programs. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to provide any additional comments or suggestions you may have.

**Section 1: General Feedback**

2. Have you participated in any training or development programs in the past 6 months? (Yes/No)

3. What motivated you to participate in training or development programs? (Select all that apply)
	* To improve job performance
	* To learn new skills
	* To stay up-to-date with industry trends
	* To advance in my career
	* Other (please specify)

**Section 2: Program Effectiveness**

1. How would you rate the relevance of the training and development programs to your job responsibilities? (1 = Not relevant at all, 5 = Very relevant)

2. Have you noticed any changes in your job performance or skills after participating in a training or development program? (Yes/No)

3. Which of the following best describes the impact of training and development programs on your work? (Select one)
	* Improved job performance
	* Increased confidence
	* Better understanding of company processes
	* Enhanced teamwork skills
	* Other (please specify)

**Section 3: Program Satisfaction**

1. How satisfied are you with the instructors or trainers who delivered the training and development programs? (1 = Very dissatisfied, 5 = Very satisfied)

2. Were the training and development programs well-organized and easy to follow? (Yes/No)

3. Did you feel that the training and development programs were worth your time and effort? (Yes/No)

**Section 4: Suggestions and Improvements**

Here is a questionnaire on Training and Development Programs:

**Training and Development Programs Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
The purpose of this questionnaire is to gather your opinions and experiences regarding the Training and Development Programs offered by our organization. Your feedback will help us improve and tailor our programs to better meet the needs of our employees.

**Section 1: Overall Satisfaction**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how satisfied are you with the current Training and Development Programs offered by our organization?

(1 = Very Dissatisfied, 2 = Somewhat Dissatisfied, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Somewhat Satisfied, 5 = Very Satisfied)

2. Have you participated in any Training and Development Programs in the past 12 months? If yes, please specify the program(s) and your level of satisfaction with it/them.

**Section 2: Program Content and Relevance**

1. Which of the following training topics would you like to see more coverage on in our organization's Training and Development Programs? (Select all that apply)

* Leadership and Management
* Communication Skills
* Technical Skills (e.g. software, tools, etc.)
* Time Management and Productivity
* Team Building and Collaboration
* Other (please specify)

2. How relevant are the current Training and Development Programs to your job responsibilities and performance goals?

(Scale: 1 = Not at All Relevant, 2 = Somewhat Relevant, 3 = Very Relevant, 4 = Extremely Relevant)

**Section 3: Delivery Methods and Scheduling**

1. What is your preferred method of learning for Training and Development Programs? (Select all that apply)

* In-person training sessions
* Online courses or webinars
* On-the-job training
* Mentorship or coaching
* Other (please specify)

2. How would you rate the scheduling of our Training and Development Programs?

(Scale: 1 = Very Poor, 2 = Poor, 3 = Average, 4 = Good, 5 = Excellent)

**Section 4: Support and Resources**

1. Do you feel supported in your professional development by our organization's Training and Development Programs?

(Scale: 1 = Strongly Disagree, 2 = Disagree, 3 = Neutral, 4 = Agree, 5 = Strongly Agree)

2. How would you rate the availability of resources (e.g. materials, equipment, etc.) for Training and Development Programs?

(Scale: 1 = Very Poor, 2 = Poor, 3 = Average, 4 = Good, 5 = Excellent)

**Section 5: Additional Feedback**

1. What do you think our organization could do to improve its Training and Development Programs?

2. Are there any specific Training and Development Programs or topics that you would like to see added or changed in the future?

3. Any additional comments or suggestions about our Training and Development Programs?

Thank you for taking the time to provide your feedback! Your input is invaluable in helping us shape the future of our Training and Development Programs.

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's a questionnaire on WorkLife Balance:

**WorkLife Balance Questionnaire**

**Introduction:**
We're interested in understanding your experiences and perceptions of WorkLife Balance at our company. Your responses will help us identify areas for improvement and create a more supportive work environment. Please answer the questions honestly, and feel free to elaborate on your responses.

**Section 1: General Perceptions**

1. On a scale of 1-5, how would you rate your current WorkLife Balance?
	* 1 (Very Poor)
	* 2 (Poor)
	* 3 (Neutral)
	* 4 (Good)
	* 5 (Excellent)

2. Do you feel that your work responsibilities interfere with your personal life? (Select all that apply)
	* Often
	* Sometimes
	* Rarely
	* Never

3. How often do you find yourself working outside of regular working hours (e.g., evenings, weekends)?
	* Daily
	* Several times a week
	* Occasionally
	* Rarely
	* Never

**Section 2: Time Management and Prioritization**

4. How do you prioritize your work and personal tasks?
	* I prioritize work tasks first, then personal tasks
	* I prioritize personal tasks first, then work tasks
	* I prioritize tasks based on urgency and importance
	* I don't prioritize tasks, I just do what comes first

5. Do you feel that you have enough time for personal activities and hobbies?
	* Yes
	* Sometimes
	* Rarely
	* Never

6. How do you manage your workload and tasks to avoid feeling overwhelmed?
	* I delegate tasks to others
	* I prioritize tasks and focus on one thing at a time
	* I use tools and apps to stay organized
	* I don't use any specific methods, I just get it done

**Section 3: Support and Resources**

7. Do you feel supported by your manager and colleagues when it comes to WorkLife Balance?
	* Yes
	* Sometimes
	* Rarely
	* Never

8. Are there any company resources or programs that support WorkLife Balance that you're aware of? (Select all that apply)
	* Flexible work arrangements (e.g., telecommuting, flexible hours)
	* Employee wellness programs (e.g., fitness classes, mental health support)
	* Employee assistance programs (e.g., counseling, financial planning)
	* Other (please specify)

9. Would you like to see more resources or programs offered to support WorkLife Balance? If so, what would you like to see?

**Section 4: Open-Ended Questions**

10. What do you think is the biggest challenge you face in achieving a good WorkLife Balance?

11. Are there any changes you'd like to see in our company's policies or culture to support WorkLife Balance?

**Thank you for taking the time to complete this questionnaire! Your feedback is invaluable in helping us create a better WorkLife Balance for everyone.**

	* Somewhat Disagree
	* Strongly Disagree

	* 25% work-related tasks and 25% personal activities

	* Occasionally
	* Rarely
	* Never

	* Somewhat Agree
	* Neither Agree nor Disagree
	* Somewhat Disagree
	* Strongly Disagree

	* Positively
	* Negatively
	* No impact

	* Yes
	* No
	* Undecided

	* Frequently
	* Occasionally
	* Rarely
	* Never
